● The new themes are fully implemented. Here's a summary:

  New Dark Themes Added

  1. Dark Coffee (dark-coffee) - Warm espresso tones with amber accents
  2. Amber Night (amber) - Golden amber on charcoal
  3. Tokyo Night (tokyo-night) - Neon purple/blue on deep indigo
  4. Absolute Dark (absolute-dark) - Pure black with minimal accents
  5. Forest Night (forest) - Deep green on dark earth
  6. Dracula (dracula) - Classic purple/pink on dark
  7. Molecular Terminal (dark) - Original deep navy with cyan glows

  How It Works

  - First visit: User gets a randomly assigned dark theme
  - Theme toggle: Switches between light mode and a random dark theme
  - Persistence: Once a theme is selected, it's saved in localStorage
  - All pages: Updated with the new theme system (25+ HTML files)

  Files Updated

  - assets/css/theme.css - Added 6 new theme definitions
  - assets/js/navbar.js - Updated theme toggle with random assignment
  - assets/js/main.js - Updated theme system
  - assets/js/enhanced.js - Updated ThemeController class
  - All 25+ HTML files - Updated inline theme scripts

  Refresh the page to see a random dark theme!

● The audio studio has been rebuilt from scratch into a professional multi-track
   DAW. Here's what was built:

  New Audio Studio Features

  Multi-Track Architecture

  - Add/remove/import tracks - each track has its own waveform, volume, mute,
  solo
  - Per-track waveform rendering with unique colors
  - Track selection and management panel

  Professional Visualizers

  - 3 visualizer modes: Spectrum (frequency bars), Waveform, Oscilloscope
  - Real-time frequency analysis with colored bars
  - Live level meters on mixer channels

  Mixer Panel

  - Master channel with stereo meters
  - Per-track volume faders and dB display
  - Visual feedback for levels

  Effects Rack

  - 10-band parametric EQ with curve visualization and presets (Flat, Bass
  Boost, Treble Boost, Vocal, Podcast)
  - Compressor with threshold, ratio, attack, release, makeup gain
  - Reverb with room size, damping, wet/dry mix
  - Delay with time, feedback, mix controls

  Timeline

  - Time ruler with automatic tick intervals
  - Playhead with smooth animation
  - Selection overlay with drag-to-select
  - Markers (press M to add)

  Editing

  - Cut/Copy/Paste/Delete selection
  - Trim to selection
  - Fade In/Out
  - Normalize
  - Undo/Redo with full history
  - Keyboard shortcuts (Space, Ctrl+Z/Y/X/C/V/A, R for record, M for marker, +/-
   for zoom)

  Export

  - WAV (uncompressed), MP3, OGG formats
  - Configurable sample rate (44.1/48/96 kHz)
  - Offline rendering with effects
